224b7(phal chen): ston to// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ nor bu rin po che chen po yid bzhin gyi rgyal po ma gtogs par lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser las lhag par 'phags pa gang yang
224b8(phal chen): med do// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes nor bu rin po che chen po yid bzhin gyi rgyal po mi gtogs par/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi
225a1(phal chen): gser las lhag par khyad par du 'phags pa gang yang med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ klu'i tshogs grub par 'gyur ba'i sbrul 'dul ba
225a2(phal chen): ni klu dang sbrul thams cad la dbang sgyur ro// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i nan tan gyi klu'i dkyil 'khor grub pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sbrul 'dul
225a3(phal chen): ba yang nyon mongs pa'i klu dang sbrul thams cad la dbang sgyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ dpa' bo lag cha dang ldan pa ni dgra'i 'khor gyis tshugs par dka'// de bzhin
225a4(phal chen): du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i lag dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyang nyon mongs pa'i dgra'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis thub par
225a5(phal chen): dka'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ lha rdzas kyi can/ ngan sbrul gyi snying po'i phye ma srang gcig gis ni stongagasum gi 'jig rten gyi khams dri zhim pos rgyas par
225a6(phal chen): 'geng ste/ den cig tsam la yang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po ches yongs su gang bas rin du ma chog go// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems
225a7(phal chen): bskyed pa lha rdzas kyi tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po lhag pa'i bsam pa gcig la gnas pa'i khams kyang / chos kyi dbyangs thams cad yon tan gyi dri zhim pos rgyas par 'gengs te/ slob pa
225a8(phal chen): dang / mi slob pa dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sems kyang zil gyis gnon to// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ tsan dan rin po che chen po kha ba'i tsan dan zhes bya ba ni gdung
225b1(phal chen): thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed de/ lus thams cad kyang rab tu bsil bar byed do// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i kha ba'i tsan dan rin po che yang nyon mongs
225b2(phal chen): pa'i kun tu rtog pa dang / 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug ga gdung ba thams cad kyang rab tu sel to// ye shes kyi lus kyang rab tu sim par byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ 
225b3(phal chen): dper na/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi drung du ji snyed cig nye bar 'dong ba de dag thams cad kyang gser gyi kha dogs sa 'gyur ro// de bzhin du gang su'ang rung ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
225b4(phal chen): du sems bskyed pa dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i drung du nye bar 'ongs pa de dag thams cad kyang / thams cad da mkhyen pa nyid kyi kha dog ca 'a ga par 'gyu ro// rigs kyi bu
225b5(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ dper na/ shing sus kyang mi chug pa dang kun nas 'du ba'i shun phrags kyi dri zhim po 'byung ba de lta bu ni/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi me tog par shi ka dang / me tog dza/ 
225b6(phal chen): ti dang / me tog sum na la sogs pa me tog gi rnam pa thams cad la'ang med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i sa bon las byung
225b7(phal chen): ba'i smon lam gyi shing gi yon tan dang / ye shes kyi shun phrags kyi dri zhim po'i nged 'byung ba de lta bu ni dge ba'i rtsa ba dma' ba dang ldan pa thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang
225b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi me tog par shi ka dang / me tog 'ja ti dang / me tog su ma na'i tshul khrims dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / shes rab dang / rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol
226a1(phal chen): pa'i ye shes mthong ba zag pa med pa dang ldan pa thams cad la'ang med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing sus kyang mi thub pa dang / kun nas 'dug pa
226a2(phal chen): 'bus par gyur na/ me tog stong phrag mang po'i 'byung gan su gyur par shes par bya'o// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i shing kun nas 'du ba dge ba'i rtsa bas
226a3(phal chen): kha 'bus par gyur na/ lha dang mi grangs med pa'i byang chub kyi me tog zag pa dang bcas pa dang / zag pa med pa'i skye gan su 'gyur bar shes par bya'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper
226a4(phal chen): na/ shing kun nas 'du ba'i me tog gis nyi ma gcig tu bsgos pa'i gos sam/ tal mar las dri zhim po'i dngad 'byung ba de lta bu yong me tog tsam pa ka dang / me tog
226a5(phal chen): sum nas nyi ma brgya phrag stong du bsgos pa'i gos sam/ til mar las kyang mi 'byung ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems kyi rgyud tshe gcig tu yongs su
226a6(phal chen): bsgos pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan dang / ye shes kyi dri zhim po'i ngad phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhabs kyi drung du ldang ba de lta bu ni bskal pa brgya phrag stong du bsgos pa'i nyan
226a7(phal chen): thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sems las kyang zag pa med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang chos kyi ye shes kyi dri zhim po mi 'byung ngo // rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing gi rig
226a8(phal chen): na li ke re zhes bya ba rgya mtsho gnod pa dang bral ba nas skye ba yod do// de'i rtsa ba yan chad me tog gi bar du yang dus thams cad du nam du yang sems can rnams kyi nye bar 'tshe bar mi 'gyur ba
226b1(phal chen): med do// de bzhin du snying rje chen po dang / smon lam gyi rtse ba yang dag par skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang thog ma thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa nas nye bar bzu
226b2(phal chen): ba phyin chad dam pa'i chos gnas pa'i mthar thug gi bar du nam yang lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi nye bar 'tsho bar mi 'gyur ba med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ dngul chu'i
226b3(phal chen): rigs gser du snang ba zhes bya ba yod do// de ni srang gcig gis kyang lcags srang stong gser du 'gyur ro// dngul chu srang cig po de ni lcags srang stong po des zad par bya ba'am/ lcags
226b4(phal chen): su bsgyur bar mo nuso// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i ro'i khams dge ba'i rtsa dab yongasu bsngos pa'i ye shes kyis bzung ba ni las dang
226b5(phal chen): nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i lcags thams cad zad par bya/ sa te/ chos thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi kha dog tu byed kyang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed
226b6(phal chen): pa'i ro'i khams gcig po de ni/ las dang nyon mongs pa'i lcags thams cad kyis kyang kun nas nyon mongs par bya ba 'am/ zad par mi nuso// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na// 
226b7(phal chen): me ni ji tsam du chung ngu zin kyang rkyen ji tsam dang phrad pa de tsam gyi me lce yongasu skyed do// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me ji tsam du chung ngu zin kyang dmigs pa rgya
226b8(phal chen): chen pos tshogs kyi rkyen ji tsam dang phrad pa de tsam du ye shes kyi 'od 'phro ba rab tu dgye bas rnam par 'phel bar byed// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ me mar cig las me mar bya ba brgya phrag
227a1(phal chen): stong zhig bus kyang / me mar de ni de snyed byung bas ma zad de mthar thug pa med do// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me mar gcig las
227a2(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du thugs bskyed pa'i me mar mang po 'bar yang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du
227a3(phal chen): sems bskyed pa'i me mar gcig po de ni de snyed kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me mar byung bas mi zad de mthar thug pa med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ me mar
227a4(phal chen): gcig cig khyim 'am khang bu ji lta bur bcug kyang rung ste/ bcug ma thag tu lo stong du bsags bsags pa'i mun da yang rnam par sel cing snang bar byed// de bzhin du thams
227a5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa'i sems bskyed pa gcig kyang sems can gyi bsam pa'i khyim thibs po ma rig pa'i mun pa dang ldan ba ci lta bu yang rung ste/ de'i rgyud tu byin/ de phyin ma thag tu bskal pa
227a6(phal chen): brgya stong brjod du med par bsags pa'i las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / mun pa thams cad rnam par sel cing ye shes kyi snang ba yongasu skyed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ me mar ni snying
227a7(phal chen): po ji tsam pa de'i rkyen tsam du snang bar byed de/ mar gyi tshogs ji srid du gnas pa de srid du 'bar ro// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i me mar yang / byang chub sems dpa'i
227a8(phal chen): smon lam gyi snying po'i khyad par ci 'dra ba de lta bur chos kyi dbyings yongasu snang bar byed de/ snying rje chen pos spyod pa'i mar gyi tshogs ji srid du gnas pa de srid du/ sems can gdul ba dang / 
227b1(phal chen): zhing yongasu dag par bya 'a dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku don bsgrub pa la yongs su 'bar bar gnas so// / shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas
227b2(phal chen): bal po che zhes bya ba las sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/ bam po brgya bcu gsum pa/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ lha rdzas kyi 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi rgyan lha
227b3(phal chen): rgyal po dbang sbyor gyi mgo la thogs pa ni/ 'dod pa la spyod pa'i lce'i bu thams cad kyis mi 'phrog so// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa lha rdzas kyi 'jam bu chu klung / 
227b4(phal chen): gser gyi rgyan nan tan dang / yon tan la rab tu gnas pa byang chub sems dpa' phyir mi ldog pa rnams kyi sgo ngan lam chen po'i mgo la thogs pa ni/ byis pa tha dad pa'i
227b5(phal chen): skye bo dang / slob pa dang / mi slob pa dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs so// rigs kyi 'di lta ste dper na/ ririgs kyi rgyal po seng ge'i nga ros na seng
227b6(phal chen): go'i phra gu skyes nas ring po ma lon pa'ang nyam su bde zhing rta'i ri dgas thams cad ni kun tu 'byer bar 'gyuraro// de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa skyes bu'i seng ge chen po'i thams cad mkhyen pa
227b7(phal chen): nyid kyi nga ro byang chub kyi sems yongs su rjod pa phyung bas ni/ las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i phru gu rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos kyis nyams su bde zhing rta'i dmigs pa la
227b8(phal chen): gnas pa'i sems can thams cad ni kun tu 'byor ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ seng ge'i rgyus pa las rgyud tu byas pa'i pi bang gi sgras na po bang thams cad kyi rgyud yongasu 'chang
228a1(phal chen): de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sku mngar ba'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i rgyas pa'i yon tan brjod pa'i sgras 'dod pa'i rgyud kyi ga
228a2(phal chen): ba'i pobang thams cad kyi rgyud yongs su 'chad par 'gyur ro// nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa dang / yon tan gyi gtam thams cad kyang yongs su 'gag par 'gyur ro// rigs
228a3(phal chen): kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rgya mtsho chen po ba dang ma he dang ra'i 'o mas yongs su gang ba'i nang du seng ge'i 'o ma thigs gcig blugs pas/ 'o ma de dag thams cad 'gyes par
228a4(phal chen): 'gyur te 'dur mi btub bo// de bzhin du bskal pa brgya phrag stong du bsags pa'i nyon mongs pa kun gyi 'o ma'i rgya mtshor yang de bzhin gshegs pa skyes bu'i seng ge
228a5(phal chen): chen po'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i / ma'i thigs pa gcig blugs pas thams cad ma lus par zad par 'gyur te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs
228a6(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par thar pa rnams kyang mi gnas mi 'du'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ bya ka la bing ka'i phru gu sgo nga'i sbubs nas ma byung ba la nga ro'i mthu'i khyad
228a7(phal chen): par yod pa de lta bu ni gangs kyi ri la gnas pa'i bya'i tshogs mthu dang shugs thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa thams cad la yang med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' ka la bang
228a8(phal chen): ka ri phru gu las dang po pa 'khor ba'i sgo nga'i sbubs na 'dug pa la snying rje chen po dang / byang chub kyi sems kyi nga ro'i mthu'i khyad par yod pa de lta bu ni/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs
228b1(phal chen): rgyas thams cad la med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ na mkha' lding chen po'i phru gu skyes nas ring po ma lon pa la gshog pa'i rlung gi stobs dang / mthu bdog pa
228b2(phal chen): dang / mig yongasasu dag pa'i yon tan yod pa de lta bu ni/ de ma yin pa'i bya lus tshad du phyin pa gzhan thams cad la'ang med do// de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa
228b3(phal chen): na mkha' lding chen po'i rigs dang / rgyud du byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa' na mkha' lding chen po'i phru gu sems dang po bskyed pa la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems
228b4(phal chen): bskyed pa'i gshogs pa'i rlung gi stobs dang / shugs bdogs pa dang / snying rje chen po dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa'i mig yongasu dag pa'i yon tan
228b5(phal chen): yod pa ni nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas bskal pa ba rgya stong tshang bas byung ba thams cad la med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ skyes bu chen po'i
228b6(phal chen): lag nas sprad pa'i mde'u thung gis ni go tsa ji tsam du sra yang brtol to// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus brtan po dang ldan pa'i lag nas spyad pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
228b7(phal chen): du sems bskyed pa'i mde'u thung gis kyang lta ba dang bag la nyal ba'i go cha thams cad mi brtol ba med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ mthu bo che chen po khros te rngam pa'i 'phel
228b8(phal chen): bal thor bu ji srid du gnas pa de srid du 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi thams cad kyis kyang mi thub bo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' mthu bo che chen po snying rje chen pos rngam pa'i lhag pa'i
229a1(phal chen): bsam pa'i gdong la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i thor bu ji srid du gnas pa de srid du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs

229a3(phal chen): goms pa la 'phong gi gnas dang / thabs kyi mthu dang / khyad par bdog pa de lta bu ni thams cad la byang yang 'phong mi shes pa rnams la med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems
229a4(phal chen): dpa' cang shes las dang po pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sa la goms pa la smon lam gyi ye shes dang mos dpas spyod pa'i mthu'i khyod par ci bdog pa de lta bu ni/ 
229a5(phal chen): byang chub tu sems ma bskyed pa'i sems can thams cad dang / slob pa dang / mi slob pa dang / rang sangasargyas thams cad la med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ 
229a6(phal chen): dper na/ 'phong slob pa'i 'phong gi rgyus thams cad la ni dang por rkang pa'i stangs la goms par bya ba la sngon du 'gro'o// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
229a7(phal chen): kyi sa la slob pas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad khong du chud par bya ba la yang dang por thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa la yang dag par gnas pa sngon
229a8(phal chen): du 'gre'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i mkhan po sgyu ma'i rnam pa dang / yul thams cad yongasu ston pa'i bya ba thams cad ni dang por sngags kyi dngos grub mngon par bsgrub pa
229b1(phal chen): yid la byas na/ 'grub par 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i yul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu ston pa'i sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'

230b1(phal chen): kyis mi 'chi'o// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i bdud rtsi'i chu 'thungs pa yang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sar mi

230b3(phal chen): rnam par spyod kyang mi kun gyis mi mthong ngo // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i shes rab dang / smon lam gyis nye bar brtan pa bdud kyi yul thams cad la/

230b5(phal chen): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa chos kyi rgyal po chen po brten pa yang sgrib pa dang bar chad dang ngan song thams cad kyis mi 'jigs
230b6(phal chen): so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ sa phug gi khyim na gnas na/ sa'i gseb thams cad rlan kyis yongasu gang bas me'i 'jigs pa med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems kyi rgyud byang chub
230b7(phal chen): kyi sems kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas mngon par brlan pa la'ang nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi rnam par grol ba'i ye shes kyi mes 'jigs pa med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ dpa'
230b8(phal chen): bo la rten pa'i mi ni dgra thams cad kyis mi 'jigs so// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa dpa' bo la rten pa yang spyod pa ngan pa'i dgra thams cad
231a1(phal chen): kyis mi 'jigs so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin rdo rje'i lag cha thogs pa ni/ lha ma yin gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu 'jom
231a2(phal chen): mo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa brtan pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa rdo rje'i lag cha thogs pa yang bdud dang phas kyi rgol ba'i lha ma
231a3(phal chen): yin gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu 'jom mo// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rtsi ro'i bcud 'thungs pa'i skyes bu ni tshe shin tu ring bar gnaso// nyam chung bar mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin
231a4(phal chen): du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i ro'i bcud kyi tshegs 'thungs pa yang bskal da pa grangs med par 'khor ba na 'khor yang yongasu skyo ba med
231a5(phal chen): la 'khor ba skyon gyis mi gos so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na/ sman gyi ro sbya ro cog thams cad du chu ni sngon du 'gro ba ste/ gang la yang skyon tu mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du
231a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / smon lam gyi tshogs sbyar ba thams cad du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa na sngon du 'gro ste/ gang la yang skyon tu mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu
231a7(phal chen): 'di lta ste dper na/ mi'i don du bya ba thams cad la ni srog gi dbang po sngon du 'gro'o// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par blang ba la'ang byang
231a8(phal chen): chub kyi sems sngon du 'gro'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ skyes bu srog gi dbang po dang bral ba ni las thams cad la mthu med pas pha ma dang / gnyen bshes kyi tshogs kyis
231b1(phal chen): kyang nye bar 'tshe bar byar med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa dang bral ba yang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thob par bya ba la mthu med
231b2(phal chen): bas/ sems can thams cad kyis kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi yon tan gyis nye bar 'tsho ba rabyar ming ngo // rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rgya mtsho chen po ni dug thams cad kyis gdug/ 
231b3(phal chen): par mi nus so// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rgya mtsho chen po yang las dang nyon mongs pa dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas su sems bskyed pa'i dug
231b4(phal chen): thams cad kyis gdug par mi nus so// rigs kyi bu 'di de lta ste dper na/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor na sker ma tham das cad kyi 'od kyis thub par mi nus so// de bzhin du thams
231b5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i nyi ma'i dkyil 'a ra yang nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi skar ma thams cad kyi yon tan zag pa med pa'i 'od kyis mi thub
231b6(phal chen): bo// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rgyal po'i bu skyes nas yun ring du ma lon pa yang / blon po'i mchog tu bya ba nas rgan pa thams cad rig su rigs dang ldan par skyes pa
231b7(phal chen): dang dbang gis zil gyis gnon to// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub tu sems bskyed nas ring po ma lon pa/ chos kyi rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su
231b8(phal chen): skyes pa'i las dang po pa yang / yun ring po nas tshangs par spyod spyod pa'i nyan thos nas rgan pa thams cad byang chub kyi sems kyi snying rje chen po'i dbang gis zil kyis
232a1(phal chen): gnon to// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ blon po ji tsam du rgan pas kyang rgyal bu gzhon nu ji tsam du chung ba'a'ang phyag bya dgos// rgyal por
232a2(phal chen): bus kyang blon po rgan po la rim gro mo bya ba ma yin no// de bzhin du nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas ji tsam du rgan la/ ji tsam du tshangs pa'i spyod pa ring du spyod spyod pa rnams kyis kyang / 
232a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa la gdung byer bya'o// byang chub sems dpas kyang nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas rnams la rim gro med par bya ba ma yinon// rigs kyi bu 'di
232a4(phal chen): sto dper na/ rgyal po'i bu thams cad kyis mi dgos pabya ba zhig na'ang rgyal po'i mtshan dang ldan na/ rigs dkyis btsun pas rgyal po'i blon po dam par bya ba thams cad
232a5(phal chen): dang yang mi mnyamo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' las dang nyon mongs pa'i nye bar len pa thams cad kyis non pa yang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed
232a6(phal chen): pa'i mtshan dang ldan na/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyi btsun zhing che bas nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas mchog tu phyin pa thams cad dang yang mi mnyamo// rigs kyi bu 'di ltas
232a7(phal chen): dper na/ nor bu rin po che yong su dag pa ni mig la rab rib kyi skyon yod na yongs su ma dag par snang ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rin po che rang
232a8(phal chen): bzhin gyis yong su dag pa yang sems can dad pa'i mig mi shes pa'i rab rib kyi skyon dang ldan pa rnams la yongasu ma dag par snang ngo // rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rtsi'i gzu
232b1(phal chen): sngags dang rtsi thams cad bsdus te byas pa ni rig gam mthong ngam 'grogs na yang sems can gyi nad rab tu zhi bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub kyi sems kyi sems kyi smon lam dang / 
232b2(phal chen): ye shes kyi lus dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs dang / shes rab dang / thabs kyi sngags dang / rtsi thams cad las bsgrubs pa byang chub kyi sems dang ldan pa ni/ thos sam mthong
232b3(phal chen): ngam 'grogs sam rjesu dran pa'i tshul gyis kyang sems can gyi nyon mongs pa'i nad rab tu zhi bar byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ gos dang pa'i mtshan nyid can ni 'dam
232b4(phal chen): gyi nyes pa thams cad kyis mi gos so// de bzhin du byang chub kyi sems kyi gos dang pa'i mtshan nyid can ni 'khor ba'i nyon mongs pa'i 'dam gyi skyon thams
232b5(phal chen): cad kyis kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyuraro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing gi gzugs mgo gzer gyis btab pa ni yongasu 'gyes par mi 'gyur te bya
232b6(phal chen): ba thams cad kyang byed do// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du smon pa'i ye shes kyi lus kyi spyi bo byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i smon lam gyi gzer gyis btab pa yang byang
232b7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i bya ba thams cad la mthu yod do// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi smon lam gyi ye shes las lus su grub pa yin pas yongasu 'gyes par mi 'gyuraro// rigs kyi bu 'di
232b8(phal chen): lta ste dper na/ gzer dang mi ldan pa'i 'khrul 'khor ni shing gi yan lag de nyid yin yang dgos pa bya ba'i mthu med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du
233a1(phal chen): sems bskyed pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa dang mi ldan na/ byang chub kyi yan lag gi tshogs de nyid yin yang / sangs rgyas kyi chos bsgrub pa la
233a2(phal chen): mthu med do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po la rin po che a ga ru nag po'i glang po'i snying po zhes bya ba yod pa des bdugs ma thag tu rgyal po
233a3(phal chen): 'khor los sgyur ba'i yan lag bzhi pa'i dpung gi tshogs thams cad kyang na mkha' la gnas par 'gyur ro// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa a ga rus
233a4(phal chen): bdugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams/ cad kyang khams gsum pa thams cad las rnam/ bar 'das te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes
233a5(phal chen): nam mkha'i spyod yul 'dus ma byas pa thams cad kyi mthar thug par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni rin po che ma rabs kyi 'byung kung nas mi
233a6(phal chen): 'byung gi/ rdo rje'i 'byung kung 'am/ gser gyi 'byung kung nas 'byung ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje lta bu'ang sems can gyi bsam pa'i
233a7(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba ma rabs kyi rin po che'i 'byung gnas nas mi skye ste/ gzhan du na sems can yongasu skyob pa'i snying rje chen po'i rdo rje'i 'byung kung 'am/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye
233a8(phal chen): shes la lhag par dmigs pa'i gser gyi 'byung kung chen po nas 'byung // rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ shing gi rigs rtsa ba med pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de'i rtsa ba mthar thug pa
233b1(phal chen): mi dmigs mod kyi/ shing rnams la yal ga dang / lo ma dang / mdab ma dang / me tog shin tu rgyas pa dra ba lta bur gyur pa snang ngo // de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed
233b2(phal chen): pa'i rtsa ba'i mthar thugs pa'ang mi dmigs mod kyi/ 'jig rten gyi skyed gnas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bsod nams dang / ye shes dang / mngon par shes pa'i me tog shin tu rgyas pa
233b3(phal chen): smon lam chen po'i dra bar gyur pa'ang yongasu snang ngo // rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni snod ngan pa'i gzhi la 'dug na mdzes par mi snang ngo // snod ma rdol ba ma gtogs par snod rdol pa
233b4(phal chen): dang bu ga can gyis gzung bar mi nuso// de bzhin du thams ca mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa'i rdo rje chen po ya dang sems can mos bzhan pa'i snod dang / ser sna can nam/ 
233b5(phal chen): tshul khrims ngan pa can nam/ gnod sems can nam/ le lo can nam/ dran pa 'khrugs pa'am/ shes rab 'chal ba'i rnams la mi mdzes te/ byang chub sems
233b6(phal chen): dpa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa rin po che'i snod ma gtogs par sems can lhag pa'i bsam pa log pa la zhugs pa blo mi brtan pa'i snod kyis kyang gzung bar mi nuso// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste
233b7(phal chen): dper na/ rdo rje ni rin po che thams cad 'bug so// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje yang sangs rgyas kyi chos rin po che thams cad phugs par khong du chud bar
233b8(phal chen): byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje ni brag thams cad shigs par 'jom mo// de bzhin du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rdo rje yang lta ba'i rnam pa thams cad

234a8(phal chen): dang mi'i lag tu phyin par mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rin po che yongasu brtag pa la mi mkhas pa'i skyes bu ni rdo rje rin po che'i yon tan nyam su myong bar mi 'gyur

235b8(phal chen): cad nye bar ston pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa byed pa dang / chos kyi sprin chen po yong su 'dzin pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs dang / shugs dang / 
236a1(phal chen): drag shul de dag kyang gzhan dun thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed ba smon lam thams cad kyi ye shes rdo rje sra pa'i lte ba can ma gtogs par/

236b1(phal chen): ces smras so// 'phags pa pho brang brtsegs pa'i chab sgo dbyer gsol nang du mchi'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' byams pas khang pa brtsegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan

236b3(phal chen): pab brtsegs pa 'dir song shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs ngo mtshar chen po thob par gyur te/ khang pa brtsegs pa de'i nang du phyin pa dang / byin ma thag tu sgo de yang rang chad
236b4(phal chen): par gyur to// des mthong ba khang pa brtsegs pa de shin tu rgya che zhing yangs la/ rgyar dpag tshad brgya stong mang po dang ldan pa na mkha'i dbyangs kyi tshad kyis gzhal ba/ 
236b5(phal chen): 'khor thams cad du na mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan gyi rgyan grangs med pas brgyan/ rin po che grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis
236b6(phal chen): brgyan pa/ mu tig gi phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu sbyangs pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu sbyangs pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ mu tig dmar po'i phreng
236b7(phal chen): bgrangs med pa rab tu sbyangs pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan po/ seng ge'i mu tig gi phreng ba grangs med pa rab tu sbyangs pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ seng ge'i rgyal mtshan grangs med pa'i rgyan
236b8(phal chen): kyis brgyan pa/ zla ba dang zla gam grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ dar gyi lnga ldi sna tshogs grangs med pa rab tu sbyangs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ dar gyi ba dan sna tshogs grangs med pa'i
237a1(phal chen): rgyan gyis brgyan ga/ rin po che mang po grangs med pa'i 'od kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser gyi dra ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i snam bu grangs
237a2(phal chen): med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser gyi lcags bod rin po ches spras pagrangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ dril bu sgra snyan pa 'byung ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa rin po
237a3(phal chen): che'i dril bu g.yer ka'i dri ba bskyod na yid du 'ong ba'i sgra 'byung ba grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ lha rdzas kyi me tog mang po'i char mngon par 'bab pa grangs med pa'i brgyan gyis
237a4(phal chen): brgyan pa/ lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i lde ldi mngon par sbyangs pa dgrangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gam yo nas spos kyi snod nas bdug spos 'thul ba'i yo byad grangs med
237a5(phal chen): pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ gser phye ma'i char rab tu 'ang ba pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ pu sha dra ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ skar kung grangs
237a6(phal chen): med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ rta babs grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ ba gam grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ me long gi dkyil 'khor grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan
237a7(phal chen): pa/ rin po che'i phag gu grangs med pa gtams pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i rtsig pa grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rini po che'i ka ba grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis
237a8(phal chen): brgyan pa/ rin po che'i gos kyi sprin grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i shing grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i khri 'phang grangs med pa'i rgyan gyi
237b1(phal chen): brgyan pa/ rin po che'i lam grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i grangs med pa'i ba dan gyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ sa'irigani rgyan sna tshogs grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgya/ 
237b2(phal chen): pa/ rin po che'i grangs med pa las brtsigs pa'i khang pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i khri grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i grangs med pa'i rkyen gyis brgyan
237b3(phal chen): pa/ rin po che'i snam bu grangs med pa btang ba'i 'chag sa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi chu shing gi ka ba shin tu rnam par phye ba grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan
237b4(phal chen): pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi gzugs grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus grangs da med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ bya'i tshogs sna tshogs
237b5(phal chen): yid du 'ong ba'i sgra 'byin pa grangs med pa'i rkyen kyis brgya na pa/ rin po che'i pad+mo grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i srog shing 'dzin pa grangs med pa'i// / 
237b6(phal chen): rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rdzing bu grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ me tog pun 'da' ri ka grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che'i them skas grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ 
237b7(phal chen): rin po che'i stegs bu rnam par bkod pa grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs grangs med pas spras pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ nor bu rin po che chen po'i 'od grangs
237b8(phal chen): med pa rab tu 'gyed pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che thams cad rnam par phye ba grangs med pa'i rgyan kyis brgyan pa/ yon tan dang legs pa phun sum tshogs pa grangs med pa'i
238a1(phal chen): rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ 'dug par mthong ste/ khang pa brtsegs pa de'i nang na yang khang pa brtsegs pa gzhan brgya stong 'di lta bu'i rgyan gyis/ lhab lhub kyis brgyan
238a2(phal chen): pa/ rin po che'i gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang lha'i ba dan grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa nas/ yon tan dang legs pa phun sum tshogs pa grangs med pa'i bar gyi rgyan gyis brgyan pas
238a3(phal chen): gang bar mthong ngo // khang pa brtsegs pa de dag thams cad kyang de ltar rgya che zhing yangs pa/ de ltar tshad med de na mkha'i mdzod du gyur pa/ kun nas shin tu sba bar 'khod par mthong // 
238a4(phal chen): des khang pa brtsegs pa rnam par phye ba de dag thams cad kyang dmigs pa gcig la phan tshun ma 'dres pa dang // phan tshun ma 'dzings pa dang / phan tshun sa la sal por
238a5(phal chen): 'dug par gzugs brnyan gyi tshul de de la snang bar gyur te/ dmigs pa gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du dmigs pa ma lus pa de dag thams cad la'ang snang bar mthong ngo // 
238a6(phal chen): de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis khang pa brtsegs pa chen po rnam par snang mdzad kyi rgyan kyis brgyan pa'i snying po'i yul dang / rnam par 'phral ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam pa
238a7(phal chen): de lta bu dag mthong nas/ dga' ba'i shugs dpag tu med pa rnam par 'phel ba'i spro ba dang / mos pa chen pos lus dang sems mngon par brlan pa dang / 'du shes kyi rnam pa thad
238a8(phal chen): rnam par bsal ba'i yid dang / sgrib pa thams cad rnam par bzlog pa'i sems dang / rmongs pa thams cad dang rnam par bral ba dang / 'khrul pa med pa'i phyogs la rab tu gnos
238b1(phal chen): ba dang / sgra thams cad la thogs pa med pa'i dran pas rnam par dmigs pa'i rna ba dang ldan pa dang / yid la bya ba'i rnam par 'khrug pa thams cad bral ba dang / rnam par thar pa
238b2(phal chen): sgrib pa med pa'i tshul gyi rje su 'brang ba'i blo dang / dmigs pa thams cad la sgrib pa med par mig rab tu 'gro bar gyur nas/ phyogs kyi rgyud thams cad la mngon du ltas pa'i lus
238b3(phal chen): kyi phyag bya bar mngon par bsgrub pa'i stobs thams cad du khyab pa dang ldan pa'i lus thams cad kyis phab ste phyag byaso// de ltar tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis phyag byas
238b4(phal chen): ma thag tu/ byang chub sems dpa' byams pa'i byin gyi rlab sa kyi mthus khang pa brtsegs pa de dag thams ca/ da kyi nang du bdag nyid phyin par shes par gyur to// khang
238b5(phal chen): pa brtsegs pa de dag thams cad du'ong rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yul can rnam pa sna chog sa rnam pa tha dad pa mngo po yang mthong bar gyur te/ khang pa
238b6(phal chen): brtsegs pa la lar ni/ byang chub sems dpa' byams pas thog ma rigs ni gang du skyes te/ mang ci zhes bya bar gyur pa zhig gis dge ba'i rtsa ba gang dang / yongasu bskul ba gang dang / 
238b7(phal chen): dge ba'i bshes gnyen gang gis yang dag par bskul ba dang / tshe'i tshad ni ji tsam zhig tu/ bskal ba'i ming na tse zhes bya bar/ de bzhin gshegs pa ni gang la rgyan ni ji lta bu zhig dang
238b8(phal chen): ldan pa'i zhing du 'khor na ji lta bu zhig tu/ smon lam gyi khyad par ni ji lta bu zhig mngon par bsgrubs te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam gyi sems bskyed pa
239a1(phal chen): de dag thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur to// shes par gyur to// khong du chud par gyur to// de'i tshe sems can de dag dang / de bzhin gshegs pa de'i sku tshe'i tshad dang / 
239a2(phal chen): tshe'i tshad ji srid cig tu gyur pa de tsam gyi du su/ de bzhin gshegs pa de'i zhabs kyi drung na bdag nyid 'dug par yang shes par gyur te/ bya ba de dag thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur to// khang
239a3(phal chen): babartsegs pa la lar ni byang chub sems dpa' byams pas thog ma gang du byams pa'i ting 'dzin thob par gyur pa dang / dus gang nas bzung ste/ de'i mang byams pa zhes bya bar gyur pa de
239a4(phal chen): ngag mthong bar gyur to// la lar ni gang du spyod pa spyad pa dang / da la lar ni gang du pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu rdzogs pa dbyas pa dang / la lar ni gang du bzod pa la zhugs pa dang / 
239a5(phal chen): lar ni gang dus non pa dang / la lar ni gang du sangs rgyas kyi na nga gi rgyan yongasu bzung ba dang / la lar ni gang du nga bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa yongasu bzung ba dang / la la
239a6(phal chen): ni gang du mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par gyur pa dang / la lar ni gang du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bstan pa dang / rnam pa ni ji lta bu zhig lung bstan pa dang / 
239a7(phal chen): lung na sus bstan pa dang / yun na ji srid gcig gis lung bstan pa de dag thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur to// khang pa brtsegs pa la lar ni byang chub sems dpa' byams pa 'khor
239a8(phal chen): los sbyar ba'i rgyal por gyur te/ sems can rnams dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la rab tu 'gad pa mthong bar gyur to// la lar ni 'jig rten gyi mgon por gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi phan ba dang / 
239b1(phal chen): bde ba thams cad kyis sems can rnams la nye bar sdud pa dang / la lar ni brgya byin du gyur te/ 'dod pa'i yon tan gyi dga' ba las sems can rnams rnam par zlog pa dang / la lar ni tshangs par
239b2(phal chen): gyur te/ bsam gtan dang / tshad med pa'i dga' ba sems can rnams la yongasu rjod pa dang / la lar ni lha'i dbang po rab mtshe mar gyur te/ tshad med pa'i yon tan sems can rnams la yongs su
239b3(phal chen): rjod pa dang / la lar na lha'i dbang po rab dga' ldan du gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' tshe gcig gis thogs pa'i yon tan rjod pa dang / la lar ni lha'i rgyal po rab tu 'phrul dga' bar gyur te/ lha'i
239b4(phal chen): 'khor du byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sprul pa'i rgyan yongasu ston pa dang / la lar ni lha'i rgyal po dbang sgyur du gyur te/ lha rnams la chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba yang
239b5(phal chen): dag par ston pa dang / la lar ni bdud du gyur te/ lha rnams la phun sum tshogs pa thams cad mi rtag par ston bri/ dang / la lar ni lha ma yin gyi dbang po'i gnasu skyes te/ lhan
239b6(phal chen): yin gyi 'khor na nga rgyal dang / dregs pa dang / rlom pa thams cad rab tu spang ba dang / ye shes kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'jug par bya ba dang / chos kyi ye shes kyi sgyu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston pa
239b7(phal chen): mthong ngo // khang pa brtsegs pa la lar ni gshin rje'i 'jig rten mthong bar gyur te/ de na byang chub sems dpa' byams po 'od kyis sems can dmyal ba thams cad snang bar byed cing / 
239b8(phal chen): sems can dmyal bar skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa mthong // khang pa brtsegs pa la lar ni yi dgas kyi gnas
240a1(phal chen): mthong bar gyur te/ de na byang chub sems dpa' byams pa sems can yi dgas kyi gnas skyes pa rnams la kha zas dang btung ba mang ngo nye bar sgrub cing bkres pa
240a2(phal chen): dang skom pa rab tu zhi bar byed pa mthong ngo // khang pa brtsegs pa la lor ni byol song gi skye gnas na skye ba'i skye mched rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs kyis byol song gi skye gnasu gtogs pa
240a3(phal chen): sems can mang po 'dul po mthong ngo // khang pa brtsegs pa la lar ni rgyal po chen po'i khamasu gtogs pa'i lha'i 'khor na 'jig rten gyi mgon po rnams la chos bston pa mthong //

249a4(phal chen): du 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas mchod pa la sems can yongasu skul pa dang / spos dang byug pa gsol zhing 'bru mar gyi dro zhim pos byug pa dang / dril bu dang me tog
249a5(phal chen): ge 'bring ba gsol ba la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas mchod pa rnam pa thams cad la brtson pa dang / dang ba bcu'i las kyi lam la sems can rab tu 'god pa dang / 
249a6(phal chen): bslab pa'i gnas lnga dang / gso sbyin gyi yan lag brgyad dang / sangs rgyas dang / chos dang dge 'dun la skyabs btsal ba dang / rab tu 'byung ba dang / chos mnyan pa dang / lung mnod/ 
249a7(phal chen): ba dang / kha thon bya ba dang / tshul bzhin yid la bya ba la sems can 'god par byed pa dang / chos kyi gtam bya ba'i phyir seng ge'i stan la 'dug cing / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub rnam
249a8(phal chen): par 'grel pa dang / de ltar byang chub sems dpa' byams pas bskal pa bye bo khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa ro pha rol tu phyin pa drug la spyad pa de dag thams cad tshong dpon gyi
249b1(phal chen): bu nor bzangs kyis/ mig mangs ris de dag las rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan mthong bar gyur to// des khang pa brtsegs pa la la las ni byang chub sems dpa' byams pas dge ba'i
249b2(phal chen): bshes gnyen ji snyed cig bsnyen bkur ba de dag thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur te/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen de dag thams cad kyi drung du
249b3(phal chen): bdag nyid phyin cing / tshur shog nor bzangs legs par 'ongs sam/ mingal lam/ 'di re byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'di dag la ltos shig ces sgo zhing
249b4(phal chen): gtam byed par shes par gyur te/ de ltar tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis khang pa brtsegos pa de dag re re dang / dmigs pa de dag re re las kyang bsam gyis mi
249b5(phal chen): khyab pa'i rgyan dang / yul rnam par sprul pa 'di dag dang / gzhan dag kyang grangs med pa mang po mthong bar gyur te/ dran pa'i mthu nyams pa med pa dang / mig
249b6(phal chen): yong su dag pa phyogs kun tu rnam par lta ba dang / lhag mthong la lta ba'i ye shes sgrib pa med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes dang / byin gyis rlabs kyi dbang rab
249b7(phal chen): tu thob pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'du shes kyi rnam pa la zhugs pa'i ye shes kyi sa la gnas te/ mtha' yas pa'i rgyan dang / yul rnam par sprul pa de dag thams cad
249b8(phal chen): mthong bar gyur to// 'di lta ste dper na/ skyes bu gnyid kyis log pa'i rmi lam du gzugs kyi dmigs par khyad par sna tshogs mang po zhig mthong bar gyur to// 'di ltar

250a2(phal chen): rab dang / dka thub kyi nags tshal mdangs dga' ba'am/ shing dang chu klung dang rdzing dang ri mdangs dge' ba'am/ ges dang khazas dang btung ba'i langs spyod nyam su bde ba 'am/ glu dang
250a3(phal chen): sal sran dang ral mo'i sgra snyan pas tshogs kyis rtse ba nyamasu dga' bzhig mthong ngam/ ba ma dang gnyen bshes dang bdag nyid 'grogs par shes par gyur pa'am/ rgya mtsha chen 'ang
250a4(phal chen): rgyal por rab dang / lha'i gnas thams cad ngam/ 'jam/ dbu'i gling dag na bdag dpag tshad brgya phrag dum dar gnas par shes par gyur la khyim 'am/ gnas de'
250a5(phal chen): shin tu yangs shing yon tan dang / rgyan thams cad kyi yongs brgyan par mthong ste/ nyan par zhig yin pa rjen sa kyang nam de yang ring ba dang / thung bar bye brag mi byed
250a6(phal chen): la rmi lam yin pa tsam du'ang mi shes so// bdag nyid kyang bde ba'i yo byad thams cad dang ldan zhing / lus kyi 'du byed zo bdog bde la snyom pa dang / gnyid med de mi dga' ba thams cad
250a7(phal chen): yongasu bsal bas dga' ba dang / bde ba rgya chen po nyam su myong ste/ yun kyang ring mo zhig lon bstan nas nyin gcig gam/ nyin bdun nam/ zla ba phyed dam/ zla ba gcig gam

250b2(phal chen): dang ldan par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'du shes kyi rnam pa yangs shing che ba dang / sgrib pa med pa la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa'i rgyan gyi yul khong du chud la/

250b7(phal chen): yi dgas kyi yul lam/ gshin rje'i mi log ca gnyems pa thogs pa gshe zhing khro ba dag kyang mthong bar gyur/ sems can dmyal ba pa'i dud mo dang / 'o dod kyi sgra yang thos
250b8(phal chen): par gyur la ba tsa'i chu de dag mthong ste/ spu gri'i so bshibs pa'i ri de dag dang / lcags kyi shal ma la'i sdong po de dag dang / ral gra'i so'i nags tshal de dag kyang mthong bar gyur tam/ 
251a1(phal chen): sems can dmal ba de dag kyang kun nas 'bar zhing yongasu 'bar ba dang / rab tu 'bar ba dang / lcags kyi bum pa gcig tu 'bar ba de dag kyang mthong bar gyur la
251a2(phal chen): gnod pa de dag thams cad kyis kyang gnod par bya zhing / tshor ba de dag kyang nyam su myong ba tsam du shes par gyur te/ sems can dmyal ba de dag kyang me'i gdung bas sdug bsngal ba
251a3(phal chen): zhig tu mthong ngam/ bdag gis myong bar gyur tam/ las dge ba'i tshogs kyis lha'i khang pa dang / gnas shig mthong bar gyur tam/ lha'i 'khor dang / lha mo'i tshigs dang /

251a5(phal chen): gyi shing dang / longs spyod mang po mthong ngam/ nyam su myong bar gyur te/ tshe'i yun kyang de dang mnyam bar shes par gyur na/ de ni 'di nas kyang 'phos pa med
251a6(phal chen): der yang skyes pa med do/ mi snang bar ma gyur bzhin du/ las kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pas bya ba'i rnam pa de lta bu dag shes shing mthong la nyamasu myong bar rung // de bzhin

251a8(phal chen): lta ste dper na/ skyes bu 'byung po'i gdon gyis non pa ni/ gzugs kyi rnam pa sna tshogs mang po mthong ste/ ci dris pa de dag gi lung yang ston to// de bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu

251b7(phal chen): bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis kyang / rgyan de dag thams cad dmigs pa thams cad du phan tshun ma 'dres pa dang / phan tshun ma 'dzings par gzugs rab tu byung ba mthong ngo //
